        function openDemo(url) { var modal = document.getElementById('demo-modal'); var iframe = document.getElementById('demo-iframe'); var body = document.body; iframe.src = url; modal.classList.remove('hidden'); body.style.overflow = 'hidden'; }
        function closeDemo() { var modal = document.getElementById('demo-modal'); var iframe = document.getElementById('demo-iframe'); var body = document.body; modal.classList.add('hidden'); iframe.src = ''; body.style.overflow = 'auto'; }
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(event) { if (event.key === "Escape") { closeDemo(); } });
        let currentIndex = 0; const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.testimonial-card');
        function scrollTestimonial(direction) { if (direction === 1) { currentIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % cards.length; } else { currentIndex = (currentIndex - 1 + cards.length) % cards.length; } cards[currentIndex].scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest', inline: 'center' }); }
        function startTimer(duration, display) { var timer = duration, minutes, seconds; setInterval(function () { minutes = parseInt(timer / 60, 10); seconds = parseInt(timer % 60, 10); minutes = minutes < 10 ? "0" + minutes : minutes; seconds = seconds < 10 ? "0" + seconds : seconds; display.textContent = "00:" + minutes + ":" + seconds; if (--timer < 0) { timer = duration; } }, 1000); }
        function startTypingEffect() { const words = ["Professional", "High Conversion", "Siap Dipakai Jualan", "Terstruktur Rapi", "Hard selling"]; let i = 0; let timer; const typingElement = document.getElementById('typing-text'); if(!typingElement) return; function typingEffect() { let word = words[i].split(""); var loopTyping = function() { if (word.length > 0) { typingElement.innerHTML += word.shift(); } else { setTimeout(deletingEffect, 1000); return false; } timer = setTimeout(loopTyping, 100); }; loopTyping(); } function deletingEffect() { let word = words[i].split(""); var loopDeleting = function() { if (word.length > 0) { word.pop(); typingElement.innerHTML = word.join(""); } else { if (words.length > (i + 1)) { i++; } else { i = 0; } typingEffect(); return false; } timer = setTimeout(loopDeleting, 50); }; loopDeleting(); } typingEffect(); }
        function scrollToEmoji(e) { e.preventDefault(); const target = document.getElementById('scroll-cue'); if (target) { target.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }); } }
        window.onload = function () { var tenMinutes = 60 * 10; var display = document.querySelector('#countdown'); startTimer(tenMinutes, display); startTypingEffect(); const stepContainer = document.querySelector('.js-step-container'); const stepLine = document.querySelector('.js-step-line'); const stepNumbers = document.querySelectorAll('.js-step-number'); const stepCircles = document.querySelectorAll('.js-step-circle'); const stepImages = document.querySelectorAll('.step-image'); if (stepContainer && stepLine) { stepLine.style.transition = 'none'; stepLine.style.transformOrigin = 'top'; function updateLineProgress() { const rect = stepContainer.getBoundingClientRect(); const windowHeight = window.innerHeight; const totalDistance = windowHeight + rect.height; const distancePassed = windowHeight - rect.top; let progress = distancePassed / totalDistance; progress = Math.max(0, Math.min(1, progress)); stepLine.style.transform = `scaleY(${progress})`; const totalSteps = stepNumbers.length; const activeIndex = Math.floor(progress * totalSteps); stepNumbers.forEach((num, index) => { if (index <= activeIndex) { num.classList.remove('text-gray-400'); num.classList.add('text-gradient-step'); if(stepCircles[index]) { stepCircles[index].classList.add('step-circle-active'); } if(stepImages[index]) { stepImages[index].classList.add('step-image-active'); const imgInside = stepImages[index].querySelector('img'); if(imgInside) imgInside.style.opacity = '1'; } } else { num.classList.add('text-gray-400'); num.classList.remove('text-gradient-step'); num.style.webkitTextFillColor = 'initial'; if(stepCircles[index]) { stepCircles[index].classList.remove('step-circle-active'); } if(stepImages[index]) { stepImages[index].classList.remove('step-image-active'); const imgInside = stepImages[index].querySelector('img'); if(imgInside) imgInside.style.opacity = '0.9'; } } }); } updateLineProgress(); window.addEventListener('scroll', updateLineProgress, { passive: true }); } const stickyCta = document.getElementById('sticky-cta'); const tutorialSection = document.getElementById('tutorial'); const offerSection = document.getElementById('offer'); window.addEventListener('scroll', () => { const scrollY = window.scrollY; const windowHeight = window.innerHeight; const tutorialTop = tutorialSection.offsetTop; const offerTop = offerSection.offsetTop; const showThreshold = tutorialTop - windowHeight + 300; const hideThreshold = offerTop - windowHeight + 200; if (scrollY > showThreshold && scrollY < hideThreshold) { stickyCta.classList.remove('hidden-sticky'); } else { stickyCta.classList.add('hidden-sticky'); } }); };
    </script>

<!-- Script Logic Notifikasi -->
<script>
    (function() {
        // Fungsi Helper untuk menghasilkan waktu yang bervariasi secara acak
        function getRandomTime() {
            const rand = Math.random();
            
            // 30% Kemungkinan muncul "Baru saja"
            if (rand < 0.3) {
                return "Baru saja";
            } 
            // 50% Kemungkinan muncul "X menit lalu" (1 - 59 menit)
            else if (rand < 0.8) {
                const minutes = Math.floor(Math.random() * 59) + 1;
                return `${minutes} menit lalu`;
            } 
            // 20% Kemungkinan muncul "X jam yang lalu" (1 - 2 jam)
            else {
                const hours = Math.floor(Math.random() * 2) + 1;
                return `${hours} jam yang lalu`;
            }
        }

        // Data Dummy (Relevan dengan Pengguna Landing Page Engine)
        const buyers = [
            { name: "Andi Pratama", job: "Digital Creator" },
            { name: "Siti Aminah", job: "Owner UMKM" },
            { name: "Budi Santoso", job: "Software Developer" },
            { name: "Rina Marlina", job: "Freelance Designer" },
            { name: "Eko Kurniawan", job: "Online Marketer" },
            { name: "Dewi Sartika", job: "Content Creator" },
            { name: "Fajar Nugraha", job: "Dropshipper" },
            { name: "Putri Ayu", job: "Virtual Assistant" },
            { name: "Rizky Hidayat", job: "Mahasiswa" },
            { name: "Dimas Anggara", job: "Graphic Designer" },
            { name: "Doni Setiawan", job: "Course Creator" },
            { name: "Maya Sari", job: "Affiliate Marketer" }
        ];

        const container = document.getElementById('social-proof-container');

        function createNotification() {
            // Ambil data random
            const buyer = buyers[Math.floor(Math.random() * buyers.length)];
            // Generate waktu random saat notif dibuat
            const timeAgo = getRandomTime();
            
            // Buat elemen notif
            const notif = document.createElement('div');
            notif.className = 'pointer-events-auto bg-white border border-gray-200 shadow-lg rounded-xl p-3 flex items-start gap-3 w-[300px] max-w-[85vw] notif-enter relative overflow-hidden';
            
            notif.innerHTML = `
                <!-- Aksen Orang di Kiri -->
                <div class="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 bg-brand-500"></div>
                
                <!-- Avatar -->
                <img src="https://ui-avatars.com/api/?name=${buyer.name.replace(' ', '+')}&background=f97316&color=fff&size=64" alt="Avatar" class="w-10 h-10 rounded-full border-2 border-white shadow-sm shrink-0">
                
                <!-- Konten Teks -->
                <div class="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p class="text-xs text-gray-500 font-medium mb-0.5 flex items-center gap-1">
                        <svg class="w-3 h-3 text-green-500" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 20 20"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M10 18a8 8 0 100-16 8 8 0 000 16zm3.707-9.293a1 1 0 00-1.414-1.414L9 10.586 7.707 9.293a1 1 0 00-1.414 1.414l2 2a1 1 0 001.414 0l4-4z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg>
                        <span>Pembelian Berhasil</span>
                    </p>
                    <h4 class="text-sm font-bold text-gray-900 leading-tight">${buyer.name}</h4>
                    <p class="text-[10px] text-gray-500 truncate">${buyer.job}  ${timeAgo}</p>
                </div>
                
                <!-- Tombol Close -->
                <button onclick="this.parentElement.remove()" class="text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 transition-colors p-1 -mt-1 -mr-1">
                    <svg class="w-4 h-4" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12"></path></svg>
                </button>
            `;

            container.appendChild(notif);

            // Hapus notif setelah 3 detik tampil (SESUAI PERMINTAAN)
            setTimeout(() => {
                notif.classList.remove('notif-enter');
                notif.classList.add('notif-exit');
                
                // Hapus dari DOM setelah animasi keluar selesai (0.5s)
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (notif.parentElement) {
                        notif.remove();
                    }
                }, 500);
            }, 3000);
        }

        // Jalankan fungsi pertama kali (delay 2 detik)
        setTimeout(() => {
            createNotification();
            
            // Loop setiap 20 detik (SESUAI PERMINTAAN)
            setInterval(createNotification, 20000);
        }, 2000);

    })();
</script>
